Because he destroyed the temple of the Bearing race, the Oneness Sky Palace must be under a lot of pressure. Zen didn't want to cause any more troubles for the palace.

"You are quite gracious," Winchell said as he looked at Zen with admiration. If it was him in this position, he probably wouldn't be willing to hand them over.

Hearing this, Goran snorted. He said, "For many years, the Oneness Sky Palace was bullied by the Bearing race. This time, you subdued them with your own power. What can they do to us next? You got them with your efforts so naturally, they now belong to you!"

"But I'm worried that the Bearing race would seek revenge against the palace..." Zen seemed hesitant.

"For the past years, people have fought repeatedly for profit in the Source World," Athemar said after he took a sip of his tea. "A fierce war will break out sooner or later. Even if we don't provoke them, they will probably take revenge on us when that time comes. However, they might not dare take actions now."

The three masters were very open-minded about these issues. They chose their own paths and followed their own fates. It was clear to them that a mere compromise could not stop the Bearing race from fighting against the Oneness Sky Palace.

"In conclusion, you must hide your identity well on the Other Shore. Don't expose yourself to anyone, even to those who are from our palace!" Goran advised.

After the accident that occurred on the Other Shore, the Oneness Sky Palace counted the number of trapped elite disciples.

With the exception of the Vastness Mountain, all of the other six mountains had trapped elites. These included the Oneness Mountain and the Origin Mountain. Strangely enough, disciples from the Vastness Mountain were not involved. Because of this, Goran thought that not everyone from the Oneness Sky Palace could be trusted.

Zen completely understood what they meant by this. He nodded and asked, "How is Milo now?"

It was clear to Zen that he wouldn't have been able to escape from the combined attack from the Bearing race and the Divine Farmer race by himself.

Milo finally displayed an astonishing skill which allowed Zen to escape.

Without his help, the elites of the Oneness Sky Palace, including himself, would have been annihilated.

With a dark look on his face, Athemar responded, "He hasn't regained consciousness yet."

"Is his soul severely injured?" Zen sighed and asked.

During that time, Milo was completely engulfed by the Champion Fish.

How was he able to bear their ceaseless biting? "It's not because of the soul damage," Athemar shook his head as he explained.

"Then, what?" Zen asked with uncertainty.

"You must have seen the sword strike Milo made," Athemar replied.

"I did," Zen nodded.

For Zen, Milo's final strike was absolutely incredible. It directly froze all the Champion Fish and even a part of the wall.

Zen was thoroughly puzzled. Milo's Soul of Light had not yet reached the level of Indigo Soul. However, his strike was much stronger than those of ordinary Indigo Souls.

"He had utterly overdrawn his talent. Therefore, he was severely punished.

We are trying our best to revive him but it takes time," said Athemar.

Yet, Athemar didn't mention to Zen what talent Milo had overdrawn to launch that strike.

The reason why they visited Zen was to ease his worry and confirm the truth as well.

The Oneness Sky Palace would never admit that it was Zen who destroyed the temple. However, the outside world still believed that Zen had a close connection with the Oneness Sky Palace.

However, other forces wouldn't be able to blame the Oneness Sky Palace for whatever Zen did on the Other Shore. Moreover, this could also scare other super forces and warned them that whoever dared provoke Oneness Sky Palace on the Other Shore would bring tragedy to themselves.

Over the next couple days, the Bearing race negotiated with the Oneness Sky Palace. They demanded that the man who destroyed their temple return their soul crystal and Other Shore Tokens.

The Oneness Sky Palace only admitted that they indeed stopped that man from demolishing the entire temple. However, it was beyond their ability to ask him to return the soul crystal and Other Shore Tokens he took from the temple for they had no idea who that man was.

This kind of statement was almost hard to disprove. The Bearing race needed to swallow this bitter loss.

Despite their anger, they kept their word. They asked the Sun Crow race to retreat from the Mountain Viewing Province. With this, the war between the Oneness Sky Palace and the Sun Crow race ceased temporarily.

On Stage Four of the Other Shore, many Souls of Light moved back and forth through the temple of the Bearing race.

The ruins needed to be cleaned up while the collapsed beams needed to be rebuilt. For the Souls of Light in the Lust World, this was a very laborious project.

As he returned to the Other Shore with his body again, Zen headed to the temple of the Oneness Sky Palace. He wanted to get a space ring from that Thunder Beast.

For many years, that Thunder Beast stayed in the Oneness Sky Palace's temple. It was a bit apprehensive of Zen as it might be its first time to see a human body.

Nonetheless, the Thunder Beast lowered its head and stretched out its tentacles when Zen extended his hand toward it. It proceeded to make a carving around Zen's fingers.

Gradually, a shining square formed at Zen's fingertips. Just as it was about to be completely formed, it suddenly broke like a glazed tile with a sound of "bang".

"Woo?"

For a moment, the Thunder Beast appeared stunned. It never expected this to happen.

Zen was also shocked as he stared at his fingertips. He had never thought that the Thunder Beast could fail.

"Please do it again," Zen implored.

The Thunder Beast complied. It repeated the process for the second time but as soon as the space ring was almost formed, it broke again.

"Woo..."

The Thunder Beast shook its head and now refused to make a space ring for Zen the third time.

Zen's face was filled with disappointment. He turned his head and spoke to Dorothy, "It seems like the physical body is unable to get a space ring here."

Dorothy seemed relieved as she smiled and said, "Your body is invincible on the Other Shore. If you have a Sumeru Space, I'm afraid all of the good things here would be collected by you alone."

In reality, Dorothy was happy about this.

She was the only one who knew Zen's secret on the Other Shore. Zen needed her help in order to transfer those things he got on the Other Shore to his Soul of Light.

So if Zen had gotten the space ring successfully, he would not need her help anymore. Hence, she would be useless to him.

Chapter 3244 Ancestral Glory Stage Zen naturally failed to decipher what was going on in Dorothy's mind.

After he switched his form from his physical body to his Soul of Light to enter the Other Shore, he left the temple with Dorothy and headed for that square not far away.

On that square, there was a star ring. It continued to emit coldness that was chilling to the bone.

Around the star ring, many people sat with their legs crossed. They wanted to attempt at increasing their resistance against the cold.

There were many ways to improve cultivation. The privileged super forces had reserves of soul crystal, and they would absorb it to increase their cultivation of Soul of Light faster compared to others.

But the common folk in the Source World had no qualifications to enter the temples, let alone to get any soul crystal.

So they had to make use of other ways to improve cultivation that were less effective, such as enduring the brutal cold exuded by the star ring.

Since Dorothy and Zen both had Indigo Souls, they inevitably attracted a lot of attention as they approached the scene.

The Indigo Soul was invincible in Stage Four since it could reach Stage Thirteen of the Other Shore directly. As a result, Zen and Dorothy were much more compelling than the others present there.

"Let's go!"

Dorothy gestured Zen to follow after her, and then she stepped into the star ring without any hesitation.

As the star ring began to spin around her, her Soul of Light stretched up vertically and turned into a ray of light. With a swift movement, it shot up towards the sky, like a rising comet.

After Dorothy ascended, it was Zen's turn. He entered the star ring to follow after her.

Recalling back to when he first entered Stage Four, he remembered how hard it was for him to bear the pressure exerted by the same star ring.

However, that was a while ago, and his Soul of Light had made substantial progress since then. The coldness contained in the star ring could not harm him anymore.

"Whoosh!"

Within a split second, Zen had also successfully left Stage Four.

Just as they left Stage Four, a Soul of Light slowly condensed and formed in the square where they once stood.

It was the first time this soul had reached Stage Four. Naturally, he was curious about exploring his surroundings.

He glanced around to see if he could find anything worth his interest, and then he walked over to the side of the star ring. Upon noticing a warrior, he approached him and asked curiously, "Hey man, what are you guys doing here?"

The cultivator looked annoyed by his question. He glanced at him and answered impatiently, "Are you blind!? We are cultivating here!"

"What? Really?"

The man turned around and scanned the star ring with a baffled expression.

The principles of this cultivation method were not hard to understand.

Suddenly, he began to chuckle in amusement and said, "This cultivation method is equivalent to ants crawling on the ground, it's too slow! I heard that the super forces had built temples in Stage Four. Why don't you guys go there?"

Hearing his suggestion, the cultivator fell into a crippling depression. He wasn't a disciple of a noble race, which was why he didn't have the qualification to enter any of the temples. Did this man only come here to make him feel inferior and provoke him? "It's none of your business. Leave me alone!" The cultivator frantically waved his hands to drive the irritable man away.

"It's none of my business? How disrespectful! No one dared to talk to me like that in Stage Three!"

Offended by the cultivator's attitude, the man reached for his arm and gently scratched at it. As a result of this action, the cultivator's arm immediately left his torso. The man grabbed it and swallowed it down.

This man could directly devour other people's Souls of Light! What was even more shocking was that the warrior remained seated in cultivation as if he didn't sense his arm being pulled off. However, when he glanced in the direction of the man to see what he was eating, he saw it was his arm! "You, you... You can directly swallow other people's Souls of Light!" As feelings of terror filled the cultivator, he struggled with the right words to say.

"What's so strange about this? The creatures in Stage Two and Stage Three were too weak, so I came to Stage Four. This damned place. I don't like to swallow the Souls of Light of my race, but I have no choice. It seems that there are only humans in this stage?" The man replied, seeming unapologetic for his actions.

Of Course, Stage Four wasn't filled with humans only. But since they belonged to the same race, they would usually fly upwards in the same direction and land at the same location.

"What the hell is wrong with you? You're crazy!" The cultivator shrieked in horror. Then he turned into a blur and immediately retreated from the Other Shore.

"That man can actually devour Souls of Light?"

"Isn't he afraid of the consequences?"

"This guy is crazy!"

Other cultivators in the square began to scream in shock after witnessing that horrific scene.

Each soul had its own will and could not devour each other. If one devoured too many other souls, it would be overwhelmed by them and would lose control of its will.

Absorbing soul crystal was also like swallowing other souls. However, the soul crystal was not accumulated in a short time, and it was quite pure and free of such risks.

Buzz...

In the blink of an eye, all the Souls of Light in the square emptied their spots. They left out of fear of being devoured by this man.

The man looked at the empty square in disappointment and sighed, "I've said that I don't really like to devour the soul of my race. I just wanted to know how it tasted here. It seems that Stage Four is also nothing special."

He didn't bother to stop the cultivators from deserting the area. In his eyes, they were similar to insignificant ants.

There was an abundance of Souls of Light in the Other Shore. Everyone in the Source World would have their Soul of Light step onto the Other Shore once reaching the Other Shore Realm.

In addition to humans, it also harbored myriads of nonhuman creatures.

It only took the man a few days to move from Stage One to Stage Four by swallowing the Souls of Light of other beings.

While he stood still, he narrowed his eyes to look further in the distance.

Soon, his gaze fell on a temple where disciples of the Bearing race were busy with their work. A curious look appeared on his face.

'I've heard that the temples keep the purest soul crystal within them. I wonder if they would give me some if I asked.' He always did what came to his mind, nothing was stopping him this time either. With quick steps, he made his way towards the temple.

Meanwhile, Zen felt his soul take shape again. When he opened his eyes, he found he had reached Stage Five, the Primary Light Stage.

This stage was different from Stage Four. It was fully painted in white with the ground covered in layers of salt.

"Is it always so quiet in Stage Five?" Zen asked while looking around curiously.

Dorothy nodded her head and explained to him, "Most races regard Stage Four as a starting point. So Stage Five is naturally neglected. No one would stay here, unless they want to explore some unique temples."

The Other Shore Tokens of Stage Five were not much different from those in Stage Four. Moreover, those from major forces managed to obtain Other Shore Tokens from higher stages in their temples, so there was no point in exploring Stage Five.

The same could be said about Stages Six and Seven.

Zen and Dorothy didn't stay there for long. They entered another star ring and continued to ascend to the next stage.

Stage Six, the Seven-brilliance Stage, was a little dangerous and had a complex landscape. It was covered with giant rocks painted in a bright red color.

On the other hand, Stage Seven, the Nothingness Stage, was occupied by pink fern. It proved refreshing in contrast to the previous stages.

Stage Eight, the Great Ultimate Stage, seemed more like a world of only ice and snow.

Stage Nine, the Red Sun Stage, like its name, was similar to that of a blazing sun with high temperatures.

Stage Ten was called the Mysterious Light Stage...

The pair kept stepping into star rings of the stages and flying upward.

As they ascended, they felt the pressure of the star rings increase gradually.

For an ordinary person with an average Soul of Light, it would take a few years or even longer in the ascension.

However, they were Indigo Souls. They could resist the pressure with ease.

They kept progressing without a hitch.

Finally, they reached Stage Eleven, the Ancestral Glory Stage! Dozens of giant Souls of Light appeared not far from them once they showed up in Stage Eleven. These blurry Souls of Light looked terrifying, judging from the aura they emitted.

Behind Zen, there were countless star rings. No one could tell exactly how many they were.

"Humans, come this way!"

A tall and seemingly powerful Soul of Light walked up to Zen and Dorothy and pointed to the right while giving the order.

Chapter 3245 Rip Off Zen's eyes filled with confusion, his gaze switching from the star rings to the non-human creatures stationed there.

The origin of the star ring was unknown to him. All he knew was that it served as a key item for a warrior's ascension to the upper stages.

According to what he had observed, one star ring was shared among all creatures of a particular race.

For instance, despite the existence of a large number of star rings in Stage One, the human race could only rely on one to ascend to the next stage.

This was the case for all the following stages. All the humans used the same rings to ascend.

All races had their own star rings, and the star ring that belonged to the human race would normally be surrounded by humans while those that belonged to the non-human races would likewise be surrounded by nonhuman creatures.

However, the scene in front of him right now was entirely different from what he initially thought.

For one, there were countless star rings piled high before him, and two, he was being ordered around by these non-human creatures as if they owned the place! Dorothy pulled his sleeve and whispered to him. "Just do as they say."

She knew significantly more about the Other Shore so Zen chose to follow her advice, albeit with a noticeable frown on his face.

He returned his gaze onto the star rings. They had been arranged in an orderly fashion. Meanwhile, hundreds of Souls of Light gathered nearby and were lining up in two, neat queues.

"The road on your left will lead you towards the upper stage while the one on your right will lead you to the temples. Choose one and line up!" a tall, non-human creature announced in a loud voice.

A collection of various creatures immediately followed: small Ear Mice, giant beasts, and others, all lined up to form orderly queues.

"What's going on?" Zen asked Dorothy in a low voice after they joined a long line. This Stage Eleven feels different from the previous stages."

"It's because the Ancestral Glory Stage is controlled by the Separate Abyss race," she explained.

The Separate Abyss race was considered one of the strongest powerhouses in the Source World. Superior in terms of both soul and strength levels, they proved to be a force that the human race found difficulty in contending with.

Zen's eyes widened in shock upon hearing this piece of information. "A race can control an entire stage?"

"This is a special case. The Separate Abyss race is closely related to a race on the Other Shore so they got a bit of help from them in taking over this stage. Any super force that comes here would have to follow their rules,"

Dorothy told him.

"What are the rules?" Zen asked.

"Well, anyone who wants to pass through this Ancestral Glory Stage and reach Stage Twelve has to pay ten thousand soul pills. And we need to line up for our turn," she explained.

Zen turned to her with an intrigued look. "We have to pay? What if I leave Stage Twelve and go down through here? Would I still have to pay?"

Dorothy nodded. "Yeah."

She definitely knew some stuff about Stage Eleven but this was actually her first time coming here.

As a matter of fact, paying ten thousand soul pills was only to gain entry into the stage. If one wanted to explore, then they would need to pay an additional amount.

Most Souls of Light would travel up and down in the Lust World and the Separate Abyss race would charge everyone who passed this stage ten thousand soul pills as the toll.

"Isn't this robbery? What about the other large races in the Source World? Are they fine with this?" Zen asked with evident concern.

Ten thousand soul pills were nothing to an Indigo Soul, but that cost could pile up since it had to be paid every time they passed through here.

A non-human stranger snorted upon hearing his question. "The Separate Abyss race is really powerful and there's no way any other super force would be able to go against them. Besides, the cost is fairly reasonable so everyone just chooses to pay rather than causes conflict."

The stranger had a similar appearance to that of humans except for the fact that he was much shorter and had several sharp thorns on his head. Zen had no idea which race he came from but it seemed that he spoke the human language fluently.

Dorothy nodded in agreement with the stranger's words. "That's basically it."

"No wonder Emily told me that humans weren't powerful here in the Source World..."

Zen muttered to himself, feeling a bit bothered by this new information he had just learned.

To him, the Oneness Sky Palace, the Bearing race, and the Divine Farmer race were super powerful.

However, not even these three super forces combined could dream of monopolizing an entire stage. Zen couldn't help but begin to fathom just how powerful the Separate Abyss race was to have been able to do such a feat.

Zen and Dorothy waited for nearly an hour. Their turn was just about to come up when they heard a bit of a commotion up ahead. It seemed someone was begging for entrance.

"I only have eight thousand soul pills, sir. Could you please make an exception and let me pass?" The voice belonged to a human woman, very young judging from her childish tone.

"A human, eh? Don't you know the rules around here? Ten thousand pills isn't that much. If you don't have enough then you can go ahead and work over there," a Separate Abyss member guarding the place answered in spite, pointing towards the west.

The Separate Abyss race had fully occupied Stage Eleven. They had already staked their claim, erected their temples, and were actually in the process of building a grand home for them to stay in.

Construction on the Other Shore was laborious. Zen remembered the Bearing race's temple he destroyed and figured that repairing it was going to be extremely difficult and would definitely take a long time.

Since the Separate Abyss race wanted to build, then they would definitely need a lot of labourers.

The girl's lips trembled in fear when she saw the direction the guard had pointed to. Everyone knew that working under the Separate Abyss race entailed certain dangers, one of them death. There was no way she would willingly go there if she valued her life.

"I...I give up. I won't go up... I'll just go back to Stage Ten!" she exclaimed, tears brimming her eyes from disappointment.

"Of course you can go back to Stage Ten! But you'll still have to pay ten thousand soul pills if you want to leave!" The guard laughed cruelly, relishing in the devastated look that flashed upon the human girl's face.

"It's ten thousand to go up, and another ten thousand to go down. That's the rule here."

"Hahaha..."

Several more Separate Abyss members joined in, laughing at the human girl and her suffering.

Faced with such a hopeless situation, the human girl could only turn to others for help. She immediately began asking those lined up if they had two thousand soul pills to spare. She'd pay them back when she reached Stage Twelve. She promised! Unfortunately, the ones around her were all non-human creatures. Why in the world would they help her? In the end, she was left all alone.

"Then... Can I leave first and pay the debt later when I earn enough soul pills?" she asked in a soft, timid tone.

"Either pay ten thousand soul pills or go over there to work for it, girl!" the guard snapped.

With no more options left, the human girl stood there for a while before eventually walking towards the west.

It was at this time that Zen decided to step out of his spot in line. He went towards her and nodded to the Separate Abyss guard up front. "It's only two thousand soul pills. I'll pay for her."

His words shocked the human girl. She couldn't believe some stranger would be kind enough to help her out of this hopeless situation. It was a miracle! "Thank you! When I reach Stage Twelve, I promise I'll pay you back!"

Zen, however, shook his head. "No need."

He took out two thousand soul pills from his space ring and was about to give them to the guard. However, the guard merely laughed at Zen. "Boy, if you really want to help her then it'll cost you more than two thousand!"

Zen frowned. "How much would it cost?"

"One hundred thousand soul pills!" the guard declared.

Zen's face immediately darkened. These Separate Abyss members were truly determined to rip him off.

True, he had managed to acquire a lot of soul crystal from the Bearing race which made him very rich. A finger-size chunk of soul crystal could be sold for a massive amount of soul pills and a mere one hundred thousand wasn't going to cause a dent in his fortune.

What he didn't like though, was how thick-skinned the Separate Abyss race were in their dealings.

"Isn't it that everyone only has to pay ten thousand soul pills?" Zen asked in a clipped tone.

"Haha!" the guard laughed, clearly mocking Zen. "This is our place and you have to give whatever amount we ask! You want to stand up for your fellow human, then I say that both of you now have to pay one hundred thousand soul pills!"

The bystanders waiting in line could only shake their heads. This was the exact reason why nobody was willing to help the human girl earlier.

Dealing with the domineering Separate Abyss race was incredibly complicated and could end up biting them in the ass if they ever so much as offended them.

Chapter 3246 Too Greedy The exorbitant price required by the Separate Abyss race depressed the human girl as she could not afford it.

She was afraid that she couldn't leave this stage today.

Most people minded their business and would not meddle in others' affairs.

She was, thus, grateful that Zen was willing to help her. Nevertheless, two hundred thousand soul pills were simply too much.

"Fine," the girl gritted her teeth as she muttered, "I'll work for you."

Although she knew it was dangerous, she had no other choice.

At this time, Zen said, "I will pay two hundred thousand soul pills!"

The Separate Abyss race always charged at will. What was worse, they increased the price randomly. Before the guards could change their minds, Zen nodded at Dorothy.

Dorothy had been watching silently. When Zen nodded at her, she took one hundred thousand soul pills out of her space ring and offered it to the guards of the Separate Abyss race.

The human girl's eyes opened wide. Even though they didn't know each other, Zen paid such a significant sum to get her out of trouble. She was surprised and extremely grateful.

The Separate Abyss race, on the other hand, had been cunning as always.

When Zen had stepped in to help the girl, they had increased the price tenfold and asked for two hundred thousand soul pills. Nevertheless, Zen still paid that amount.

The Separate Abyss guards hadn't expected Zen to take out two hundred thousand soul pills. If they were to make things difficult for them now, it would ruin their race's reputation. Therefore, the leader of them waved his hand and said, "You can go!"

The human girl walked up to Zen and said, "I'll wait for you in Stage Twelve. Thank you for your help. I will find a way to repay you!"

Two hundred thousand soul pills were not a significant amount for any Souls of Light who could enter Stage Twelve or Stage Thirteen.

But it was an exorbitant amount for the girl as her clan had declined. As she wasn't sure whether she could acquire two hundred thousand soul pills, she was hesitant to make the promise.

"Never mind all that. You can fly upward now," Zen said with a smile.

As she was a stranger who he had met by chance on the Other Shore, Zen didn't think he would see her again in Stage Twelve. Even though he knew that she couldn't return the soul pills, Zen had still helped her.

The human girl nodded and walked toward the star ring.

Zen and Dorothy waited in line for a while before it was finally their turn.

According to the previous agreement, Zen paid one hundred thousand soul pills.

But the guard of the Separate Abyss race pointed his huge finger at Dorothy and said, "You, one million soul pills."

Dorothy's eyebrows shot up, and she asked, "Why?"

"You paid two hundred thousand soul pills for him just now. It is fair to ask you to pay a higher price," the guard said with a sneer. "If you can't afford it, go that way!"

He sneered as he pointed to the west.

"Buzz..."

Enraged, Zen's Soul of Light exuded powerful soul aura.

Even the alien races who were waiting in line felt that the Separate Abyss race was too greedy.

"They are greedy bullies!"

"That's what happens when you help others!"

"If you want to pass Stage Eleven, you have to obey them."

The other races whispered amongst themselves. They could tell that these two humans were in trouble.

"What? Do you have a problem with that?"

The guards of the Separate Abyss race glared at Zen. They didn't take him seriously.

Never before in the history of the Separate Abyss race had anyone dared to start a fight in Stage Eleven! Dorothy could feel Zen's anger, but she didn't want to cause more trouble.

She quickly interjected, "I don't have a million soul pills. Can I pay with soul crystal?"

The eyes of the guards of the Separate Abyss race lit up as soul crystal was more valuable than soul pill.

In fact, every race valued soul crystal. After all, even if you had soul pills and divine crystals, you would still be unable to exchange them for soul crystal, considering its rareness.

"It depends on how much soul crystal you are willing to pay. Ha-ha..." The guards of the Separate Abyss race laughed. As they decided who proceeded to the next stage, they used their authority to extort greater amounts.

"A finger-size chunk," Dorothy offered.

"Deal," the guards of the Separate Abyss race agreed without hesitation.

Everyone knew that soul pills could be slowly accumulated, but soul crystal was rarely seen. As they could find no way to buy some, one finger-size chunk of soul crystal was more precious than a million soul pills.

Dorothy took out a finger-size chunk of soul crystal from her space ring and handed it to the guard of the Separate Abyss race.

The other races' eyes shone with greed at the sight of the soul crystal. This was the rarely seen soul crystal. And she had actually paid the fee for passing Stage Eleven with it! What a reckless waste! Suddenly, everyone present was curious about her background.

Although they sighed with envy at the sight of the soul crystal, they cursed the Separate Abyss race. Judging from the situation, they believed that the Separate Abyss race was becoming greedier and greedier! "Let's go." Dorothy walked to Zen and tugged at his arm. She wanted to avoid trouble, but Zen was rooted to his spot. He wasn't going to allow some guards to extort such an unfair price from them.

Seeing that Zen wasn't leaving, the guards of the Separate Abyss race grinned, "Human boy, if you don't want to leave, you can stay here forever."

"Settle your anger, please. Let's go!" Dorothy pleaded with Zen.

Since staying here would only cause more trouble, Dorothy was naturally a little anxious.

Finally, Zen turned and followed Dorothy toward the star ring. As soon as their Souls of Light entered the star ring, they turned into two rays of light and flew to Stage Twelve.

The human girl had been watching the star ring all this while. She had been waiting for Zen in Stage Twelve, just as she had promised him.

She wanted to repay Zen as she owed him a big favor. But, first, she needed to know more about him, including his name.

"Buzz..."

As the two rays of light descended, Zen's and Dorothy's Souls of Light reached Stage Twelve.

"Sir, thank you..."

As soon as the human girl recognized Zen's aura, she rushed toward him.

However, before she could say more, Zen turned his head and said to Dorothy, "Wait for me here." Before anyone could object, Zen had left the Other Shore.

Dorothy's plea to stay safe and be careful echoed in the space as Zen's figure had already disappeared.

She shook her head slightly. Had the Separate Abyss race accepted two hundred thousand soul pills only, this would never have happened. But they had been unreasonable when they demanded a million soul pills. If she didn't have the soul crystal, she would have been left in Stage Eleven.

When the human girl saw Zen disappear, she was at a loss for what to do.

She stood silently for a while before she asked Dorothy, "Miss, where has he gone?"

Dorothy replied, "He'll be back soon."

She knew that it wouldn't take Zen long to turn Stage Eleven upside down.

"Oh." The human girl shuffled her feet. "Then, I'll wait for him here."

"Why are you waiting for him?" Dorothy asked as curiosity coursed through her.

"I want to know his name. I will return the soul pills to him," the girl explained.

Dorothy smiled at the girl. "You don't need to do that."

For her and Zen, two hundred thousand soul pills were not a significant amount. She did pay a higher price of a finger-size chunk of soul crystal as demanded by the Separate Abyss race, but that had nothing to do with this young human girl.

As Dorothy was generous and open-minded, she didn't blame the little girl.

"No! I must return them to him!" The girl was surprisingly persistent.

Since Dorothy's patience had waned, she said slowly, "I gave the soul pills on his behalf. Now, I'm telling you that I don't need you to pay me back.

You can leave!"

Dorothy's words upset the human girl, and she walked away reluctantly.

Chapter 3247 A Hundredfold As soon as Zen arrived—in his corporeal form—at the Oneness Sky Palace's temple, he saw a group of disciples stationed at the entrance of the temple. They all had grim expressions on their faces.

Zen quickly deduced that they were guarding against a strong enemy.

"What's the matter?"

he demanded, going straight up to one of the disciples.

Although they didn't know who he was, they knew he had helped them before.

"Before you came, something serious happened!" said the disciple, sounding frantic.

"Tell me quickly. Did the Bearing race come to make trouble again?" Zen asked, looking around him for signs of danger.

The great loss suffered by the Bearing race should have taught them not to go against the Oneness Sky Palace. Could they have dared to make trouble again so soon after their recent failure? Or was this the work of another race? The disciple shook his head. "There was a man, but he didn't belong to the Bearing race... We don't know where he came from. He can devour the souls of others!"

"A man who devours souls?" Zen repeated, startled.

"Yes!" The disciple sounded extremely upset. "He wanted soul crystal, and when we refused—he swallowed one of our members! We had to retreat to the temple."

The temple was protected by a variety of powerful restrictions. Apart from Zen, who could come and go as he pleased, even the strongest souls would be burnt to ashes.

"Then he left?" Zen asked.

"He went to the Bearing race. We think he went there for soul crystal too,"

the disciple answered.

Soul crystal was very difficult to obtain.

At the moment, there were a lot of elite disciples of the Bearing race here, but they were busy rebuilding their destroyed temple. This meant that no restrictions were yet in place to protect them. And so the man attacked them, eating at least seven souls before the rest of the members of the Bearing race fled from the Other Shore completely.

Once they were gone, the man went through the ruins of the Bearing race's temple.

However, he had come too late. The temple had already been plundered by Zen, and whatever valuables remained had also been taken away by the Bearing race. He wasn't able to find anything useful.

He refused to give up. He went next to the temple of the Divine Farmer race.

But by then, word had reached them of the danger on the Other Shore, and the temple was heavily guarded. Indeed, in the battle that ensued, the disciples of the Divine Farmer race managed to lure him inside the temple and almost succeeded in killing him. The man managed to escape the temple.

After hearing the story, Zen asked, "So where is this person now?"

"He has probably left the Other Shore. His power to devour souls is terrifying, but apart from that one ability his soul does not seem very strong.

He is also alone. He will find it hard to stand against many elite disciples united against him. When the Bearing race realized what had happened, they cooperated with the Divine Farmer race to send a few Indigo Souls to hunt him down. Unfortunately, they did not succeed in capturing or killing him," said the disciple.

"The power to devour souls... This world is so vast, so full of so many mysteries!" Zen muttered to himself, deep in thought.

That kind of power was formidable. It seemed their unknown enemy was not afraid of any kind of counterattack or adverse reaction from the souls he had devoured.

This man's Soul of Light might not be very strong now, but if he kept on swallowing souls, his cultivation speed would probably not be much slower than that of a warrior absorbing soul crystal. Zen wondered how this man had obtained such a power.

The silver lining was that at least their enemy didn't come from the Bearing race or the Divine Farmer race. Better yet, he had apparently struck a severe blow against the Bearing race.

Since Zen had learned what he needed to know, he left the temple and headed straight to the star ring. Dorothy was still waiting for him in Stage Twelve of the Other Shore.

On the way up, Zen didn't stop. He reached Stage Ten in less than an hour.

Soon after that, he stepped into the star ring again.

Several members of the Separate Abyss race stood on the square of Stage Eleven.

They had the task of driving the Souls of Light to the other side to wait in line.

With a glimmer of light, Zen's body appeared in the center of the square.

"You! This way!" one of the men shouted at Zen, coming closer to him. He was about to usher Zen into his proper place in the line when he noticed something strange. He stopped in his tracks, looking stunned. "A corporeal body?"

It was clear that the members of the Separate Abyss race had never met a corporeal body here.

Zen gave him an indifferent glance and walked past him.

The square was full of members of the Separate Abyss race, as well as people of other races who were waiting in line. One by one, as they saw Zen and realized he had a corporeal body, their faces changed and became full of shock and suspicion.

"What the hell is that?"

"This guy doesn't seem to be a Soul of Light..."

"Yes! It's simply a corporeal body!" "But how did he enter the Other Shore?"

"What is he? Is he a ghost?"

In their eyes, "ghosts" referred to souls that had left bodies. To this group, a corporeal body on the Other Shore was at least as mysterious and terrifying as a ghost in the outside.

Of course, Zen had no intention of waiting in line. He bypassed everyone and walked up to the group of people in front who seemed to be in charge.

"Excuse me, what can I do for you?" asked one of the men as Zen drew closer. The man was a member of the Separate Abyss race, and seemed to be the leader here.

Given their status in Stage Eleven, these members of the Separate Abyss race tended to have an arrogant attitude towards the new arrivals. Most of the others found them overbearing and supercilious. But Zen was unlike anyone they'd encountered here before. Faced with a corporeal body, they became polite and deferential.

Zen scowled and spoke in a threatening voice, "Repay me a hundredfold for the amount of soul pills you just took! You have charged me a million soul pills, so you must return a hundred million—otherwise, I fear this situation will not end well for you."

The Souls of Light who were waiting in line watched the scene avidly. They felt puzzled at Zen's words. They had no idea what had happened before, but right now Zen's ultimatum was very clear. He was extorting soul pills from the Separate Abyss race.

Within Stage Eleven of the Other Shore, the Separate Abyss race was the most powerful, and they were the only ones who could blackmail other races. Especially here, no one dared to fight back.

The Separate Abyss race had extorted soul pills from all the super forces and powerful people. It was rare that someone went against them. This stranger was daring.

The members of the Separate Abyss race exchanged astonished glances with each other. The truth struck them like a blow—this man in front of them was the person who had just given them soul pills and soul crystal.

The leader was silent for a moment, thinking hard. Then he said to Zen, "We apologize for failing to recognize you. If you want them back, we will return the soul crystal and the two hundred thousand soul pills you gave us." He turned to one of his companions. "Alberto, take out the soul crystal."

He and the others who were in charge of the square didn't have a high position in the Separate Abyss race. They had made a mistake in extorting Zen. Should the leader and elders of the Separate Abyss race ever learn that they had been foolish enough to offend a person capable of coming to the Other Shore in corporeal form, they would be severely punished.

They decided it would be best to avoid further trouble and just return everything to Zen.

The Souls of Light waiting in line couldn't hide their pleasure at seeing the Separate Abyss race humbled.

They who had always been so tough, who had always acted so superior, had finally met their match! Zen gave the members of the Separate Abyss race a cool glance. "No. One hundred million soul pills, or a hundred finger-size chunks of soul crystal."

The leader's face changed, and his companions looked worried.

The Souls of Light who were watching couldn't help but feel uneasy too.

What would happen if the Separate Abyss race couldn't meet the stranger's demands? They felt that something big was about to happen.

The leader squared his shoulders and glared at Zen. "Are you joking? It's enough that we will return everything to you. Alberto, hand it over."

Alberto stepped forward and gave the soul crystal to Zen. Zen grasped it in his hand, and squeezed hard.

The soul crystal burst into pieces and splattered around. Some of the fragments shot into the Souls of Light in line, and they were extremely satisfied with this unexpected development.

Without the space ring, Zen could not store soul crystal. And he did not intend to take this finger-size chunk of soul crystal.

At the waste of the soul crystal, the members of the Separate Abyss race groaned.

Zen stared coldly at them. "Send one hundred million soul pills to Stage Twelve. If there is even a single pill missing, I will raze the Separate Abyss race to the ground."

Chapter 3248 The Abyss Spirit Race Zen's statements had left everyone speechless.

Most nonhuman creatures had pinned him to be crazy. They thought he had lost his mind.

It was already a ridiculous thing for Zen to come over and blatantly demand a hundred million soul pills from the Separate Abyss race. And now he continued to assert his dominance by stating he would raze the territory of the Separate Abyss race to the ground.

Among the nonhuman creatures, there was a human. He originated from the Divine Farmer race.

This man had gone all the way from Stage Four to Stage Thirteen.

However, he had only been on the Other Shore for a short while. Therefore, he hadn't witnessed the scene of Zen destroying the temple of the Bearing race before he came here.

But he did hear from his clansmen about everything that had happened in Stage Four, including the fact that Zen could enter the Other Shore with his physical body.

"I didn't expect this brat to suddenly come to Stage Eleven. From the looks of it, the Separate Abyss race has offended him as well. Does he really plan to cause a scene in the Separate Abyss race?"

The Separate Abyss race was formidable. Their strength was not something to be underestimated. Even the Bearing race hesitated to provoke them.

Anyone who stood and watched began to anticipate the likelihood of something interesting to happen.

Upon hearing Zen's arrogant words, the leader of the guards laughed mockingly. "What did you say? You want to destroy our territory? Hahaha! What a joke!"

Initially, the Separate Abyss race wanted to come to a compromise with Zen on the issue at hand. After all, Zen was the only one who had arrived at the Other Shore with his physical body. They didn't want to offend him and cause too much trouble for either of them.

If this matter escalated without coming to a conclusion, a rumor would spread that the Separate Abyss race had demanded an exorbitant price. This would result in a severe blow to their reputation.

Now that the situation was getting out of hand, they realized the problem couldn't be solved peacefully. Therefore, they changed their attitudes.

"It's true that it's a remarkable thing to have a physical body on the Other Shore. Other races might be intimidated by you, but, we're not afraid of you!"

"I'd suggest that you move to Stage Twelve if you know what's good for you!"

"We share the same origin with the Abyss Spirit race of the Ancestral Glory Stage. Your physical body is no threat to us!"

There were many creatures of different kinds living on the Other Shore.

The strength and durability of beings increased with a higher stage.

Naturally, the ones that lived on Stage One to Stage Four were not much strong in comparison.

Some creatures would even occupy restricted areas where no one else but themselves were allowed on the Other Shore.

There was not much known about these races because they maintained a low profile. They would seldom communicate or interact with the Souls of Light. Similarly, the Souls of Light that roamed the Other Shore would never dare to enter their territories and trespass on them.

However, the Abyss Spirit race from Stage Eleven was an exception.

The Separate Abyss race and the Abyss Spirit race enjoyed a healthy relationship. It was said that in the middle ages, the Separate Abyss race was not as powerful as they stood today. When the leader of the Separate Abyss race had entered Stage Eleven, he had come across the Abyss Spirit race by chance. After a few interactions, they became exceedingly acquainted with one another.

Since the Abyss Spirit race regarded the Separate Abyss race as their allies, they supported them in all aspects of their growth in Stage Eleven. Due to their relentless assistance, the latter soon took control of Stage Eleven on the Other Shore.

It could be said that the Abyss Spirit race had made a significant contribution to their development.

"Oh, really? Is that so?"

With swift movements, Zen grabbed the arm of the man in front of him.

The immense Soul of Light was weightless in Zen's grip, and he threw him straight onto the wide square area.

Watching Zen launch a direct attack made some of the impulsive members of the Separate Abyss race charge forward to avenge their clansman.

Chaos ensued when the other races in the line saw this. They began to flee frantically in all directions like a flock of disturbed birds.

Some people took it as a source of their entertainment, while others were worried since they got involved in the matter for no reason. However, neither of them could get out of this. There was no way to retreat from the Other Shore in this damned place.

The members of the Separate Abyss race were massive in terms of size, and each of them was innate mighty warriors. Moreover, they cultivated under the watchful eyes of the Abyss Spirit race, who taught them to develop a unique soul method. It was a technique that allowed them to enhance their Souls of Light to an extended degree within a short amount of time.

At the same time, several members of the Separate Abyss race dashed towards Zen to strike. Meanwhile, Zen stood there as he had to bear terrible soul pressure from all of them.

Each of those members was equipped with a soul spear that they thrust at Zen mercilessly.

However, they had underestimated the strength and resistance of Zen's physical body.

Although they had increased their soul power substantially, a soul was still inferior to a body. Moreover, Zen's physical body was far more compelling than that of an average person.

Boom! Boom! Boom! Boom! The soul spears that would usually cause immense damage were like wooden arrows in front of Zen. The moment they came in contact with his body, they cracked into many minuscule pieces.

After a full round of countless attacks towards Zen, he remained tall on his feet completely unscathed.

Realizing that their attacks had all gone to waste, the members of the Separate Abyss race opened their eyes wide in shock. Their leader felt an undeniable fear build up inside of him.

"Alright then, it's my turn now," Zen said as he cracked his knuckles to prepare himself to counterattack.

He never was ruthless towards the people of his own race; he would show them mercy.

When he destroyed the temple of the Bearing race, he had spared the lives of all humans.

However, he didn't consider the members of the Separate Abyss race to be from his race. These intelligent beings were no different from beasts with violent tendencies.

Swish! By stomping on the ground hard with his feet, Zen boosted himself upwards as fast as an arrow released from its bow.

When he passed through a tall and mighty warrior of the Separate Abyss race, he gently pressed on his head.

Swish! The man's Soul of Light diminished in an instant! However, Zen did not plan to stop there. He turned his head to find his next target and rushed towards a man close by. Within a split second, Zen had attacked four people and destroyed their Souls of Light! "He's too strong for us!"

"We can't fight against him!"

"Hurry and inform the Abyss Spirit race!"

The remaining members of the Separate Abyss race began to retreat and flee the field one after the other. But they had nowhere to go since the area was sealed shut.

Zen stood patiently and didn't bother to follow after them to kill them off.

After observing the panicked looks on the faces of other races, he turned to them and said, "Find your own star rings and leave this place."

Without the obstruction of the Separate Abyss race, they were able to leave Stage Eleven through the star rings. And they wouldn't have to pay the heavy fee of ten thousand soul pills.

All the other races were grateful to Zen. He had helped them save ten thousand soul pills. And more importantly, he had taught the arrogant members of the Separate Abyss race a good lesson.

The Separate Abyss race had kept their dominance over small and powerless races in Stage Eleven and the Source World. It was about time someone showed up and put them in their place.

"Thank you, sir. We are grateful to you for helping us. But you have to be careful with the Abyss Spirit race!"

"Those living creatures on the Other Shore can also present themselves with their physical bodies."

"They are very powerful."

Some people who knew a little about Zen's approaching enemy gave him all the information they had so he could prepare himself.

Zen carefully listened to them and nodded. Then he made his way forward and scanned his surroundings.

The Separate Abyss race had built an entire city on the Other Shore, not just a temple. The city wall alone stood over a thousand feet high, and the buildings within were at an astounding height of ten thousand feet.

With careful steps, he walked over to the wall and gently pressed his hands against it.

As he exerted a little pressure, the wall which was one thousand feet high and one hundred feet wide collapsed with a loud sound that reverberated far and wide. A noticeable gap was formed.

The members of the Separate Abyss race, who stood behind the wall, were oblivious to the scenario that took place on the other side. They eyed Zen up in astonishment.

He had killed several of their members and the Separate Abyss race was quickly realizing how much of a threat he really was.

But they did not give up. They did not leave the Other Shore. Despite Zen's display of strength, they gathered behind him and cursed him. They wanted to stop him but did not dare approach him.

Zen had passed through another huge building a moment before its collapse.

He walked towards the center of the city, triggering the collapse of every building he passed by.

Nothing could stop him.

More and more members of the Separate Abyss race followed behind Zen.

Each time a building collapsed, their hearts sank deeper.

"Hey, human! Stop!"

"Take what you want!"

The place grew tense.

These people were not figures of authority in the city. Zen had previously asked for a hundred million soul pills, but they refused.

They had to really see Zen's power before they bowed to his wishes.

Zen ignored them profusely.

He passed a wide road where a magnificent building stood.

The building in front of him put him in even more awe. It was bigger than what he had seen before.

"What a beautiful building!"

Zen remarked.

Members of the Separate Abyss race who trailed behind him trembled at his words. They did not want to lose anything to him anymore.

"What, what do you want to do?" someone of the Separate Abyss race asked.

Zen had already destroyed the buildings in the outer part of the area, but they could not take it if he destroyed the building ahead of them. It was the real temple of the Separate Abyss race.

"I want to tear it down," Zen said nonchalantly.

Then he casually walked towards the building.

"Stop him!"

"Don't let him enter the temple!"

"Nobody can desecrate our temple!"

Members of the Separate Abyss race furiously rushed towards Zen in an attempt to stop him.

However, before they even got close, Zen shattered them instantly.

The Separate Abyss race fell into despair. Would the temple really be destroyed by a young man? Suddenly, the sound of horns played in the distance.

"Woo-oo-oo!"

Suddenly, huge eagles filled the sky. They flew from outside of the city walls carrying giants on their backs.

The giants bore a close resemblance to those from the Separate Abyss race, but the latter had blurred outlines because they were only Souls of Light.

However, the giants' appearances were clearly visible.

They were from the Abyss Spirit race that lived on the Other Shore.

"They're here to save us!"

"Kill this damn human brat!"

Excitement stirred the place. The Separate Abyss race grew confident.

Their backup finally arrived and they could smell victory coming their way.

Splash! The eagles lined up and swooped towards Zen.

The destruction of buildings was a capital offense both for the Separate Abyss race and the Abyss Spirit race. The Abyss Spirit race were definitely angered by Zen's disrespect. They were determined to kill him.

Splash! As the Abyss Spirit knights neared Zen, they revealed white bone spears in their hands.

Bone spears were known to be even more powerful than soul spears.

"Kill him!"

The Abyss Spirit knights shouted with conviction.

'How strong could these creatures from the Other Shore be?' Zen squinted his eyes as if inspecting their features.

He did not know much about the Other Shore even though he was a competent Indigo Soul now.

In his long stay on the Other Shore, he had only encountered two types of aboriginal creatures. One was the Heavenly Spider's body in the Sacred Mallow Temple, and the other was the Thunder Beast in the temple of Oneness Sky Palace.

For the first time, he encountered two creatures at the same time in the same place. One was the Abyss Spirit race, and the other was the flying eagles that they rode.

"Whoosh!"

"They seem strong.

Much powerful than Souls of Light.

But they can't be strong enough to defeat me!" Zen said scornfully.
